[]interface{}{},\n   515→\t\t},\n   516→\t\t\"title\": \"\",\n   517→\t}\n   518→\n   519→\t// Remove notPersistedProperties\n   520→\tfor prop := range notPersistedProps {\n   521→\t\tdelete(panel, prop)\n   522→\t}\n   523→\n   524→\t// Filter out properties that match defaults\n   525→\tfor prop, defaultValue := range defaults {\n   526→\t\tif panelValue, exists := panel[prop]; exists {\n  541→\t// Pass panel type information to help with threshold handling\n   542→\tpanelType := \"\"\n   543→\tif t, ok := panel[\"type\"].(string); ok {\n   544→\t\tpanelType = t\n   545→\t}\n   546→\tremoveNullValuesRecursivelyWithContext(panel, panelType)\n   547→\n   548→\t// Filter out properties that match defaults (matches frontend's isEqual logic)\n   549→\tfilterDefaultValues(panel, originalProperties)\n   550→\n   551→\t// Clean up internal markers\n   552→\tdelete(panel, \"_originallyHadTransformations\")\n   553→\tdelete(panel, \"_originallyHadFieldConfigCustom\")\n   554→}\n   555→\n   556→// filterDefaultValues removes properties that match the default values (matches frontend's isEqual logic)\n   557→func filterDefaultValues(panel map[string]interface{}, originalProperties map[string]bool) {\n   558→\t// Get panel type for panel-specific defaults\n   559→\tpanelType := \"\"\n   560→\tif t, ok := panel[\"type\"].(string); ok {\n   561→\t\tpanelType = t\n   562→\t}\n   563→\n   564→\t// PanelModel defaults from frontend\n   565→\tdefaults := map[string]interface{}{\n   566→\t\t\"gridPos\": map[string]interface{}{\n   567→\t\t\t\"x\": 0, \"y\": 0, \"h\": 3, \"w\": 6,\n   568→\t\t},\n   569→\t\t\"targets\": []interface{}{\n   570→\t\t\tmap[string]interface{}{\"refId\": \"A\"},\n   571→\t\t},\n   572→\t\t\"cachedPluginOptions\": 581→\t}\n   582→\n   583→\t// Add panel-specific defaults\n   584→\tif panelType == \"table\" {\n   585→\t\t// Remove legacy table properties (matches frontend getSaveModel filtering)\n   586→\t\t// hasAutoMigrate && autoMigrateFrom == \"table-old\" {\n   591→\t\t\t\t\tif !originalProperties[prop] {\n   592→\t\t\t\t\t\tdelete(panel, prop)\n   593→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   594→\t\t\t\t} else {\n   595→\t\t\t\t\tdelete(panel, prop)\n   596→\t\t\t\t}\n   597→\t\t\t}\n   598→\t\t}\n   599→\t}\n   600→\n   601→\t// Remove properties that match defaults, but preserve properties that were originally present\n   602→\tfor prop, defaultValue := range defaults {\n   603→\t\tif panelValue, exists := panel[prop]; exists {\n   604→\t\t\tif isEqual(panelValue, defaultValue) {\n   605→\t\t\t\t// Special case: fieldConfig - handle preservation of original custom object first\n   606→\t\t\t\tif prop == \"fieldConfig\" {\n   607→\t\t\t\t\t// Check if we need to preserve the custom object before removing ok := panelValue.(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n   611→\t\t\t\t\t\t\tif defaults, ok := fieldConfig[\"defaults\"].(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n   612→\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tif _, hasCustom := defaults[\"custom\"]; !hasCustom {\n   613→\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tdefaults[\"custom\"] = map[string]interface{}{}\n   614→\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n   615→\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t// Don't remove fieldConfig if we added custom back\n   616→\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   617→\t\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n   618→\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n   619→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   620→\t\t\t\t\tdelete(panel, prop)\n   621→\t\t\t\t} else {\n   622→\t\t\t\t\t// Only 628→\t\t}\n   629→\t}\n   630→\n   631→\t// Remove empty targets arrays (frontend removes them in cleanup)\n   632→\tremoveIfDefaultValue(panel, \"targets\", []interface{}{})\n   633→\n   634→\t// !hasFieldConfig {\n   637→\t\t\t// Recreate fieldConfig with custom object\n   638→\t\t\tpanel[\"fieldConfig\"] = map[string]interface{}{\n   639→\t\t\t\t\"defaults\": map[string]interface{}{\n fieldConfig to match frontend behavior\n   648→\tif fieldConfig, exists := panel[\"fieldConfig\"].(map[string]interface{}); exists {\n   649→\t\t// Clean up fieldConfig defaults to match frontend behavior\n   650→\t\tif defaults, hasDefaults := fieldConfig[\"defaults\"].(map[string]interface{}); hasDefaults {\n   651→\t\t\t// Remove properties that frontend considers as defaults and omits\n   652→\t\t\tcleanupFieldConfigDefaults(defaults, panel)\n   653→\n   654→\t\t\t// Preserve custom object if it was originally present, even if empty\n   655→\t\t\tif 658→\t\t\t\t}\n   659→\t\t\t}\n   660→\t\t}\n   661→\t}\n   662→}\n   663→\n   664→// isEqual checks if two values are equal (simplified version)\n   665→func isEqual(a, b interface{}) bool {\n   666→\tif a == nil && b == nil {\n   667→\t\treturn true\n   668→\t}\n   669→\tif a == nil || b == nil {\n   670→\t\treturn false\n   671→\t}\n   672→\n   673→\t// For simple types, use direct comparison\n   674→\tswitch aVal := a.(type) {\n   675→\tcase bool:\n   676→\t\tif bVal, ok := b.(bool); ok {\n   677→\t\t\treturn aVal == bVal\n   678→\t\t}\n   679→\tcase string:\n   680→\t\tif bVal, ok := b.(string); ok {\n   681→\t\t\treturn aVal == bVal\n   682→\t\t}\n   683→\tcase float64:\n   684→\t\tif bVal, ok := b.(float64); ok {\n   685→\t\t\treturn aVal == bVal\n   686→\t\t}\n   687→\tcase []interface{}:\n   688→\t\tif bVal, ok := b.([]interface{}); ok {\n   689→\t\t\tif len(aVal) != len(bVal) {\n   690→\t\t\t\treturn false\n   691→\t\t\t}\n   692→\t\t\tfor i, v := range aVal {\n   693→\t\t\t\tif !isEqual(v, bVal[i]) {\n   694→\t\t\t\t\treturn false\n   695→\t\t\t\t}\n   696→\t\t\t}\n   697→\t\t\treturn true\n   698→\t\t}\n   699→\tcase map[string]interface{}:\n   700→\t\tif bVal, ok := b.(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n   701→\t\t\tif len(aVal) != len(bVal) {\n   702→\t\t\t\treturn false\n   703→\t\t\t}\n   704→\t\t\tfor k, v := range aVal {\n   705→\t\t\t\tif !isEqual(v, bVal[k]) {\n   706→\t\t\t\t\treturn false\n   707→\t\t\t\t}\n   708→\t\t\t}\n   709→\t\t\treturn true\n   710→\t\t}\n   711→\t}\n   712→\n   713→\treturn false\n   714→}\n   715→\n   716→// cleanupDashboardForSave applies the same cleanup logic as the frontend\n   717→func cleanupDashboardForSave(dashboard map[string]interface{}) {\n 722→\tcleanupDashboardDefaults(dashboard)\n   723→}\n   724→\n   725→// removeNonPersistedProperties removes non-persisted dashboard properties\n   726→func removeNonPersistedProperties(dashboard map[string]interface{}) {\n   727→\tnonPersistedProperties := map[string]bool{\n   728→\t\t\"events\":                           true,\n   729→\t\t\"meta\":                             true,\n 760→// removeNullValues removes null values to match frontend's JSON.stringify/parse behavior\n   761→func removeNullValues(dashboard map[string]interface{}) {\n   762→\t// This handles gnetId: null   775→func cleanupTemplatingVariables(templating map[string]interface{}) {\n   776→\tif list, ok := templating[\"list\"].([]interface{}); ok {\n   777→\t\tfor _, variableInterface := range list {\n cleanupVariable cleans up individual variable properties\n   786→func cleanupVariable(variable map[string]interface{}) {\n   787→\t// Remove null datasource\n   788→\tremoveIfDefaultValue(variable, \"datasource\", nil)\n   789→\n   790→\t// Remove properties that frontend omits in getSaveModel\n   791→\tdelete(variable, \"index\")\n   792→\n   793→\t// Apply variable type-specific logic\n   794→\tif variableType, ok := variable[\"type\"].(string); ok {\n   795→\t\tswitch variableType {\n   796→\t\tcase \"query\":\n   797→\t\t\t// Query variables: keep options: [] if refresh !== never (matches frontend getSaveModel logic)\n   798→\t\t\trefresh := schemaversion.GetIntValue(variable, \"refresh\", 1) // Default to 1 (onDashboardLoad) if not specified\n   799→\t\t\tif refresh != 0 {                                            // 0 = VariableRefreshNever\n   800→\t\t\t\tif _, hasOptions := variable[\"options\"]; !hasOptions {\n   801→\t\t\t\t\tvariable[\"options\"] = []interface{}{}\n   802→\t\t\t\t}\n   803→\t\t\t}\n   804→\t\tcase \"constant\":\n   805→\t\t\t// Constant variables: remove options completely\n   806→\t\t\tdelete(variable, \"options\")\n   807→\t\tcase \"datasource\":\n   808→\t\t\t// Datasource variables: always set options to empty array\n   809→\t\t\tvariable[\"options\"] = []interface{}{}\n   810→\t\tcase \"custom\":\n   811→\t\t\t// Custom handling\n   818→\t\t\t// This is the default behavior - no additional processing needed\n   819→\t\t}\n   820→\t}\n   821→}\n   822→\n   823→// cleanupPanels cleans up panels and ensures panels property always exists\n   824→func cleanupPanels(dashboard map[string]interface{}) {\n   825→\tif panels, ok := dashboard[\"panels\"].([]interface{}); ok {\n   826→\t\t// Filter out repeated panels (matches frontend getPanelSaveModels behavior)\n   827→\t\t// Frontend filters: !(panel.repeatPanelId || panel.repeatedByRow)\n   828→\t\tfilteredPanels := []interface{}{}\n   829→\t\tfor _, 843→\t\tsortPanelsByGridPosition(filteredPanels)\n   844→\t\tdashboard[\"panels\"] = filteredPanels\n   845→\t} else {\n   846→\t\t// Ensure panels property exists even if empty (matches frontend false)\n   856→\n   857→\t\t\t// Handle nested panels in row panels\n   858→\t\t\tif nestedPanels, ok := panel[\"panels\"].([]interface{}); ok {\n   859→\t\t\t\tfor _, nestedPanelInterface := range 863→\t\t\t\t}\n   864→\t\t\t}\n   865→\t\t}\n   866→\t}\n   867→}\n   868→\n   869→// sortPanelsByGridPosition sorts panels by grid position (matches frontend sortPanelsByGridPos behavior)\n   870→func sortPanelsByGridPosition(panels []interface{}) {\n   871→\tsort.SliceStable(panels, func(i, j int) bool {\n   872→\t\tpanelA, okA := panels[i].(map[string]interface{})\n   873→\t\tpanelB, okB := panels[j].(map[string]interface{})\n   874→\t\tif !okA || !okB {\n   875→\t\t\treturn false\n   876→\t\t}\n   877→\n   878→\t\t// Get gridPos or use default values if missing\n   879→\t\tgridPosA, okA := panelA[\"gridPos\"].(map[string]interface{})\n   880→\t\tgridPosB, okB := panelB[\"gridPos\"].(map[string]interface{})\n   881→\n   882→\t\t// Default gridPos values (matches frontend PanelModel defaults)\n   883→\t\tdefaultY := float64(0)\n   884→\t\tdefaultX := float64(0)\n   885→\n   886→\t\tyA := defaultY\n   887→\t\tif okA {\n   888→\t\t\tif y, ok := gridPosA[\"y\"].(float64); ok {\n   889→\t\t\t\tyA = y\n   890→\t\t\t} else if y, ok := gridPosA[\"y\"].(int); ok {\n   891→\t\t\t\tyA = float64(y)\n   892→\t\t\t}\n   893→\t\t}\n   894→\n   895→\t\tyB := defaultY\n   896→\t\tif okB {\n   897→\t\t\tif y, ok := gridPosB[\"y\"].(float64); ok {\n   898→\t\t\t\tyB = y\n   899→\t\t\t} else if y, ok := gridPosB[\"y\"].(int); ok {\n   900→\t\t\t\tyB = float64(y)\n   901→\t\t\t}\n   902→\t\t}\n   903→\n   904→\t\tif yA == yB {\n   905→\t\t\txA := defaultX\n   906→\t\t\tif okA {\n   907→\t\t\t\tif x, ok := gridPosA[\"x\"].(float64); ok {\n   908→\t\t\t\t\txA = x\n   909→\t\t\t\t} else if x, ok := gridPosA[\"x\"].(int); ok {\n   910→\t\t\t\t\txA = float64(x)\n   911→\t\t\t\t}\n   912→\t\t\t}\n   913→\n   914→\t\t\txB := defaultX\n   915→\t\t\tif okB {\n   916→\t\t\t\tif x, ok := gridPosB[\"x\"].(float64); ok {\n   917→\t\t\t\t\txB = x\n   918→\t\t\t\t} else if x, ok := gridPosB[\"x\"].(int); ok {\n   919→\t\t\t\t\txB = float64(x)\n   920→\t\t\t\t}\n   921→\t\t\t}\n   922→\t\t\treturn xA < xB\n   923→\t\t}\n   924→\t\treturn yA < yB\n   925→\t})\n   926→}\n   927→\n   928→// cleanupRowPanelProperties removes default row panel properties that frontend filters out\n   929→func cleanupRowPanelProperties(panel map[string]interface{}) {\n   930→\tpanelType, ok := panel[\"type\"].(string)\n   931→\tif !ok || panelType != \"row\" {\n   932→\t\treturn\n   933→\t}\n   934→\n   935→\t// Remove repeat if empty string (default value)\n   936→\tremoveIfDefaultValue(panel, \"repeat\", \"\")\n   937→}\n   938→\n   939→// applyPanelAutoMigration applies the same auto-migration logic as the frontend PanelModel constructor\n   940→func applyPanelAutoMigration(panel map[string]interface{}) {\n   941→\tpanelType, ok := panel[\"type\"].(string)\n   942→\tif !ok {\n   943→\t\treturn\n   944→\t}\n   945→\n   946→\tvar newType string\n   947→\n   948→\t// Graph needs special logic as it can be migrated to multiple panels\n   949→\t// Including graphite which was previously migrated to graph in the schema version 2 migration in DashboardMigrator.ts\n   950→\t// but this was a bug because in there graphite was set to graph, but since those migrations run\n   951→\t// after PanelModel.restoreModel where autoMigrateFrom is set, this caused the graph migration to be skipped.\n   952→\t// And this resulted in a dashboard with invalid panels.\n   953→\tif panelType == \"graph\" || panelType == \"graphite\" {\n   954→\t\t// Check xaxis mode for special cases\n   955→\t\tnewType = getGraphAutoMigration(panel)\n   956→\t} else {\n   957→\t\t// Check autoMigrateAngular mapping\n   958→\t\tautoMigrateAngular := map[string]string{\n   959→\t\t\t\"table-old\":                \"table\",\n   960→\t\t\t\"singlestat\":               \"stat\",\n   961→\t\t\t\"grafana-singlestat-panel\": \"stat\",\n   962→\t\t\t\"grafana-piechart-panel\":   \"piechart\",\n   963→\t\t\t\"grafana-worldmap-panel\":   \"geomap\",\n   964→\t\t\t\"natel-discrete-panel\":     \"state-timeline\",\n   965→\t\t}\n   966→\n   967→\t\tif mappedType, exists := autoMigrateAngular[panelType]; exists {\n   968→\t\t\tnewType = mappedType\n   969→\t\t}\n   970→\t}\n   971→\n   972→\t// Apply auto-migration if a new type was determined\n   973→\tif newType != \"\" {\n   974→\t\tpanel[\"autoMigrateFrom\"] = panelType\n   975→\t\tpanel[\"type\"] = newType\n   976→\t}\n   977→}\n   978→\n   979→func getGraphAutoMigration(panel map[string]interface{}) string {\n   980→\tnewType := \"\"\n   981→\tif xaxis, ok := panel[\"xaxis\"].(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n   982→\t\tif mode, ok := xaxis[\"mode\"].(string); ok {\n   983→\t\t\tswitch mode {\n When a dashboard never originally had `defaults.custom`, the `_originallyHadFieldConfigCustom` flag is not set, causing the conditional to fail and the entire `fieldConfig` to be deleted at line 620.\\n\\n### Failure Scenario\\n1. **Input Dashboard:** Has `fieldConfig.defaults: {}` (empty, no custom) with `fieldConfig.overrides` containing `custom.displayMode` properties\\n2. **v38 Migration:** `processPanelsV38()` converts `custom.displayMode` to `custom.cellOptions` in the overrides\\n3. **Cleanup Phase:** `filterDefaultValues()` checks `_originallyHadFieldConfigCustom` flag\\n4. **Condition Fails:** Flag is not set (original input had no custom), so condition at line 608 evaluates to false\\n5. **Data Loss:** `fieldConfig` is deleted at line 620, losing all `custom.cellOptions` properties added by v38\\n6. **Result:** Dashboard loses column widths, text alignment, and other custom field configurations stored in overrides\\n\\n### What the Conditional Should Check\\nThe condition should preserve `fieldConfig` if **either**:\\n1. The panel originally had `fieldConfig.defaults.custom` (current check: `_originallyHadFieldConfigCustom == true`), **OR**\\n2. The panel currently has `defaults.custom` (added during migration) - **THIS CHECK IS MISSING**\\n\\nThe corrected logic should check if `custom` exists in the current fieldConfig structure, not just whether it existed in the original input.\\n\\n### Implementation Chain\\n1. **apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/schemaversion/migrations.go (line 74):** Registers V38 migration\\n2. **apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/schemaversion/v38.go (V38 function):** Initiates migration via `processPanelsV38()`\\n3. **apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/schemaversion/v38.go (processPanelsV38):** Processes table panels and calls `migrateOverrides()`\\n4. **apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/schemaversion/v38.go (migrateOverrides):** Converts `custom.displayMode` to `custom.cellOptions` in field overrides (adds custom properties)\\n5. **apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/frontend_defaults.go (filterDefaultValues):** Cleanup phase that incorrectly removes fieldConfig due to the flawed conditional at line 608\\n\\n### The Flawed Conditional in Context\\n```go\\n// Line 606-620 in filterDefaultValues\\nif prop == \\\"fieldConfig\\\" {\\n    // Check if we need to preserve the custom object before removing fieldConfig\\n    if panel[\\\"_originallyHadFieldConfigCustom\\\"] == true {  // <-- FLAWED LINE 608\\n        // Ensure fieldConfig structure exists with custom object\\n        if fieldConfig, ok := panelValue.(map[string]interface{}); ok {\\n            if defaults, ok := fieldConfig[\\\"defaults\\\"].(map[string]interface{}); ok {\\n                if _, hasCustom := defaults[\\\"custom\\\"]; !hasCustom {\\n                    defaults[\\\"custom\\\"] = map[string]interface{}{}\\n                }\\n                // Don't remove fieldConfig if we added custom back\\n                continue\\n            }\\n        }\\n    }\\n    delete(panel, prop)  // <-- Deletes fieldConfig when flag not set\\n}\\n```\\n\\nThe condition should be inverted or expanded to also check if `defaults[\\\"custom\\\"]` exists **in the current fieldConfig**, not just whether it existed in the original input. A corrected version would check: `if panel[\\\"_originallyHadFieldConfigCustom\\\"] == true || (current fieldConfig has custom)` before deciding to delete the fieldConfig.\\n\\n### Files and Functions Involved\\n- **apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/schemaversion/migrations.go:** `GetMigrations()` - Registers all schema migrations including V38\\n- **apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/schemaversion/v38.go:** `V38()`, `processPanelsV38()`, `migrateOverrides()` - Implements the displayMode to cellOptions conversion\\n- **apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/frontend_defaults.go:** `filterDefaultValues()` - Contains the flawed conditional at line 608 that causes field config loss\\n\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
